FNV GRAPHICS SUN WEATHER LAYOUT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which exact FNV globals and offsets expose Sky, Sun, Weather, TimeGlobals, and camera state?
2. Which offsets are valid at scene_pre_image_space, scene_post_image_space, and final_image_space?
3. Can Psycho fill sun direction, sun color, fog color, fog distance, and weather blend constants without TESReloaded?
4. Which reads are safe enough for default non-invasive mode, and which require opt-in native graphics mode?

======================================================================
EXPECTED DATA LAYOUTS TO VERIFY
======================================================================
TESReloaded/NewVegasReloaded is trusted prior art, but Psycho needs its own FNV-safe read contract.

Sky:
  Sky singleton candidate: *(Sky**)0x011DEA20
  Sky + 0x0C firstClimate candidate
  Sky + 0x10 firstWeather candidate
  Sky + 0x14 secondWeather candidate
  Sky + 0x28 sun candidate
  Sky + 0x60 sunAmbient candidate
  Sky + 0x6C sunDirectional candidate
  Sky + 0xC0 sunFog candidate
  Sky + 0xF4 weatherPercent candidate

Sun/root node:
  SkyObject/Sun RootNode candidate is expected near Sun + 0x04 or Sun + 0x08 depending on exact class.
  NiAVObject local position candidate: RootNode + 0x58
  NiAVObject world position candidate: RootNode + 0x8C
  Sun direction must be derived from a proven object transform or proven sky vector, not guessed in HLSL.

Time:
  TimeGlobals base candidate: 0x011DE7B8
  TimeGlobals + 0x0C GameHour candidate
  TimeGlobals + 0x10 GameDaysPassed candidate

Weather:
  TESReloaded source uses firstWeather/secondWeather blended by weatherPercent.
  TESWeather fog day/night near/far, sun glare, sun damage, and weather type must be proven before runtime dereference.
  Fog constants should be read or reconstructed on CPU and passed to shaders, not approximated from depth alone.

Camera:
  pCurrentCamera candidate: *(NiCamera**)0x011F917C
  Camera location globals: 0x011F426C and 0x011F474C
  Camera near/far offsets currently used by Psycho: Camera + 0xEC and Camera + 0xF0
  View/projection/inverse projection offsets still need a Ghidra-proven contract before sunshafts.
